P001 page
Common meaning:
One side of a sheet of paper, or one screen or section of a document or website.
Example:
The answer was on the next page.
RRGM bridge:
Page is bounded information surface. It holds meaning in a local field that can be turned, linked, copied, or remembered.
P002 pain
Common meaning:
Physical or emotional suffering, discomfort, or hurt.
Example:
The injury caused pain.
RRGM bridge:
Pain is harm or strain signal in the human domain. It should be noticed, not dismissed, because it can mark damage, boundary, or need.
P003 pair
Common meaning:
Two things that go together or are connected.
Example:
She bought a pair of gloves.
RRGM bridge:
Pair is two-part relation structure. It can create balance, contrast, coupling, or dependency.
P004 paper
Common meaning:
A thin material used for writing or printing, or a written document.
Example:
The paper was folded in half.
RRGM bridge:
Paper is record-bearing ES. It can preserve language, memory, proof, instruction, or claim.
P005 parent
Common meaning:
A mother, father, caregiver, or source from which something comes.
Example:
The parent helped the child cross the street.
RRGM bridge:
Parent is origin and care relation. It carries duty, protection, nurture, pressure, and source continuity.
P006 part
Common meaning:
A piece or portion of a whole.
Example:
The wheel was part of the machine.
RRGM bridge:
Part is local structure inside a larger structure. It may be small but still load-bearing.
P007 path
Common meaning:
A route, track, course, or way of moving or acting.
Example:
The path led through the forest.
RRGM bridge:
Path is movement or process structure. It connects starting condition to possible outcome through gates and transitions.
P008 pattern
Common meaning:
A repeated form, design, behavior, or recognizable structure.
Example:

RRGM bridge:
Pattern is recognition structure across repetition or relation. In DI, stable pattern can support MI continuity.
P009 pause

A temporary stop or break.
Example:

RRGM bridge:
Pause holds process without ending it. It can protect reflection, repair, boundary, or capacity.
